### [125] [FlowEdit: Associative Memory for Lifelong Pronunciation Adaptation in Flow-Matching TTS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20518)
*Harshit Singh,Ayush Pratap Singh,Nityanand Mathur*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FlowEdit 是一种针对流匹配 TTS 系统的无需微调的生命周期适应框架，通过将纠正信息存储在霍普菲尔德网络中，实现了对特定词汇发音错误的高效、实时修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的流匹配文本转语音（TTS）模型在部署后难以在线更新，导致对未登录词（OOV）或专有名词的发音错误无法快速修正，而重新训练模型成本过高。因此，作者旨在寻找一种无需微调模型参数即可实现实时发音纠正的方法。

Method: 1. 提出“生命周期适应”框架，通过学习文本嵌入空间的标记级扰动来实现发音修正。2. 利用现代霍普菲尔德网络（Modern Hopfield Network）作为可寻址的长期记忆存储修正信息。3. 在推理阶段，通过带相似度门控的软注意力机制检索修正内容，实现模糊形态匹配。

Result: 在包含18个语系、312个专有名词的基准测试中，FlowEdit 将目标词的音素错误率（PER）降低了 92.7%，同时保持了与基线模型一致的通用语音质量，且单次纠正仅需约15秒。

Conclusion: FlowEdit 为流匹配文本转语音系统提供了一种高效的持续学习方案。通过在潜空间进行修正而非微调模型权重，该方法成功实现了在保持原始语音质量的前提下，实时纠正特定词汇的发音错误，具有极高的实用价值和扩展性。

Abstract: Flow-matching text-to-speech systems achieve remarkable zero-shot quality but remain static after deployment: pronunciation errors on out-of-vocabulary proper nouns persist unless the model is retrained. We introduce FlowEdit, a life-long adaptation framework for frozen flow-matching TTS that learns pronunciation corrections as latent conditioning edits rather than weight updates. When corrective feedback is provided, FlowEdit optimizes a token-level perturbation in the text embedding space, then stores the correction in a Modern Hopfield Network serving as content-addressable episodic memory. At inference, corrections are retrieved via soft attention with a similarity gate, enabling fuzzy morphological matching. On our curated benchmark of 312 multilingual proper nouns across 18 language families, FlowEdit reduces target-word Phoneme Error Rate by 92.7% relative to the zero-shot baseline while maintaining identical general-speech quality. Corrections complete in approximately 15 seconds on a single GPU.

### [126] [DeepSWIP: Quotient-WMC Counterfactuals for Neural Probabilistic Logic Programs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20526)
*Saimun Habib,Vaishak Belle,Fengxiang He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文引入了 DeepSWIP，一种用于神经符号系统（DeepProbLog）的单世界反事实推理框架。它通过将神经感知与概率逻辑进行因果整合，实现了比传统双胞胎模型更高效、更精确的反事实推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的神经符号系统（如 DeepProbLog）主要关注联想推理，缺乏对反事实逻辑的支持。为了使神经符号系统能够处理复杂的因果干预和反事实推理，需要一种能够结合因果语义与神经感知的框架。

Method: 提出 DeepSWIP：一种单世界反事实语义。其核心方法包括：1. 神经物化（Neural Materialization）：将固定上下文的神经谓词转换为普通的 ProbLog 选择；2. SWIPs（单世界干预程序）：应用单世界干预语义；3. 加权模型计数（WMC）：在单一转换后的程序上执行 WMC 以计算反事实；4. 引入基于 AIPW（增强逆概率加权）的估计器，用于校正神经模型校准退化带来的偏差。

Result: 1. 在 MPI3D 数据集上，DeepSWIP 的推理速度比 DeepTwin 方法快 2.14 倍；2. 理论分析证明了该方法在有限接地和唯一支持模型假设下的精确性；3. 在 SUMO HOV 实验中，使用 AIPW 估计器有效消除了因神经模型校准偏差导致的估计误差。

Conclusion: DeepSWIP 提供了一种高效且精确的深度神经符号反事实推理框架。通过将神经谓词物化为标准概率逻辑程序，它不仅简化了计算，还通过处理神经网络的校准偏差，显著提升了反事实估计（如ATE）的准确性，证明了在神经符号系统中集成因果语义的可行性与优越性。

Abstract: Neurosymbolic systems such as DeepProbLog combine neural perception with probabilistic logic, but standard inference is associational. Counterfactual reasoning additionally requires a causal semantics for interventions and evidence. We introduce DeepSWIP, a single-world counterfactual semantics for DeepProbLog programs. Using neural materialization, we reduce fixed-context neural predicates to ordinary ProbLog choices, apply Single World Intervention Programs (SWIPs), and compute counterfactuals by weighted model counting (WMC) over a single transformed program. Under finite grounding and unique-supported-model assumptions, DeepSWIP is exact relative to the learned materialized FCM. The standard quotient-WMC form of ProbLog conditionals identifies active neural probabilities and explains intervention cleaning, calibration sensitivity, and rare-evidence instability. Experiments on MPI3D confirm the transformation against a DeepTwin construction against 12,000 queries, as predicted and a 2.14$\times$ inference speedup from avoiding the Twin's endogenous duplication. A SUMO HOV experiment shows that neural calibration degradation biases plug-in estimates, while a correctly scoped randomized-policy AIPW estimator removes most first-order bias for population mean and ATE estimands. Code is at https://github.com/saibib/deep_SWIP.

</details>


### [127] [LedgerAgent: Structured State for Policy-Adherent Tool-Calling Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20529)
*Md Nayem Uddin,Amir Saeidi,Eduardo Blanco,Chitta Baral*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LedgerAgent通过引入独立的任务状态“分类账”，实现了客服智能体的显式状态管理与前置合规校验，显著提升了工具调用的准确性与策略遵循能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统工具调用智能体未显式区分任务状态，依赖提示词上下文重构状态，导致智能体易因信息陈旧、丢失或错误而产生决策偏差，且难以在复杂的领域策略约束下保持合规性。

Method: 提出了LedgerAgent方法，引入独立的“分类账（Ledger）”机制来显式维护和更新任务状态。该方法将状态信息显式注入提示词中，并在执行环境变更类工具调用前，基于分类账进行策略约束检查，以拦截潜在的违规操作。

Result: 在四个客服领域及多种主流模型（开源和闭源）测试中，LedgerAgent在平均pass@k指标上优于传统的基于提示词的工具调用方法，特别是在更严格的多轮一致性指标上表现出显著优势。

Conclusion: LedgerAgent通过显式状态管理和事前策略校验，有效解决了传统工具调用智能体在复杂客服场景中面临的知识陈旧和违规调用问题，为构建更可靠、合规的智能体提供了有效范式。

Abstract: Policy-adherent tool-calling agents in customer-service domains must maintain task states across turns while calling tools and obeying domain policies. Task states consist of relevant facts, identifiers, constraints, and conditions observed through user interaction and tool calls. In standard agents, task states are not represented separately. Observations, tool returns, and policy instructions are placed in the prompt, leaving agents to reconstruct the relevant states from the prompt each time they decide what to do next. This design makes state management implicit, creating two common failure modes. An agent may retrieve the right facts but later ground its decision in stale, missing, or incorrect information; and a syntactically valid tool call may still violate a domain policy that depends on the current task state. We introduce \textsc{LedgerAgent}, an inference-time method for tool-calling agents that maintains observed task states in a separate ledger and renders the states into the prompt. The ledger is also used to check state-dependent policy constraints before environment-changing tool calls are executed, blocking policy violations. Across four customer-service domains and a mixed panel of open- and closed-weight models, \textsc{LedgerAgent} improves average pass\textasciicircum{}k over a standard prompt-based tool-calling approach, with the largest gains under stricter multi-trial consistency metrics.

### [128] [How Do Instructions Shape Speech? Cross-Attention Attribution for Style-Captioned Text-to-Speech](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20532)
*Nityanand Mathur,Hamees Sayed,Wasim Madha,Apoorv Singh,Sameer Khurana,Akshat Mandloi,Sudarshan Kamath*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本研究通过将归因分析技术引入语音扩散模型，量化了自然语言风格描述如何驱动语音生成，揭示了其在特定模型层级和采样步骤中的调控规律，填补了语音合成可解释性研究的空白。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于自然语言风格描述的语音合成（Style-captioned TTS）系统虽能控制语音特征，但其内部机制（即具体词汇如何影响声学输出）尚不明确，导致难以诊断模型缺陷及提升可控性。

Method: 提出了一种针对语音扩散模型的交叉注意力归因（Cross-attention Attribution）方法，将DAAM框架适配至语音领域。通过在CapSpeech-TTS模型中提取25个层和24个ODE步骤的逐标记热力图，分析了3600组风格描述词与文本转录组合，量化评估了风格标记对波形的影响。

Result: 研究发现：1) 风格标记的时间方差低于内容/功能标记，证实了其全局调节作用；2) 风格注意力与基频（F0）和能量高度相关；3) 风格调节在扩散过程的早期步骤和深度层中达到峰值；4) 在第17层注意力熵达到最小值，此时风格重要性达到峰值，表明模型在该阶段具有最高选择性。

Conclusion: 本研究首次揭示了自然语言如何通过交叉注意力机制影响语音扩散模型。研究表明，风格控制通过特定的层和扩散步骤实现，且网络在特定的深度呈现出最大的风格选择性，为未来开发更具可解释性和可控性的表达性语音合成系统提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Style-captioned text-to-speech systems use natural language to control voice characteristics, but how individual words influence acoustic output remains unclear. Understanding this is critical for diagnosing failure modes and improving controllability in expressive TTS. We propose cross-attention attribution for speech diffusion models, adapting the DAAM framework to the speech domain for the first time, and apply it to CapSpeech-TTS. Our method extracts per-token heatmaps across 25 layers and 24 ODE steps. We analyze 3,600 (style caption, text transcript) combinations comprising 120 style captions conditioning the generation of 30 text transcripts each, revealing how caption tokens shape waveforms. Results show: (1) style tokens have lower temporal variance than content/function tokens, confirming global conditioning; (2) style attention correlates with F0 and energy; (3) style conditioning peaks in early steps and deep layers; (4) attention entropy reaches its minimum at layer 17, co-occurring with the style importance peak, indicating maximal network selectivity at the most style-critical stage. This is the first study of how natural language influences cross-attention in speech diffusion models

</details>


### [129] [Toward Calibrated Mixture-of-Experts Under Distribution Shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20544)
*Gina Wong,Drew Prinster,Suchi Saria,Rama Chellappa,Anqi Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文探讨了混合专家（MoE）模型在分布偏移下的校准问题，指出软路由模型需要额外的校准机制，并提出了一种基于对抗性重加权的训练方法以优化模型的预测可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 虽然在个体预测器层面进行校准（如MoE模型）能提升准确性和校准度，但目前关于该策略在何种条件下有效以及在分布偏移环境下如何表现的研究尚不充分。

Method: 研究人员分析了混合专家（MoE）模型在分布偏移下的路由机制与专家级校准之间的关系，并提出了一种针对路由聚合校准误差的对抗性重加权（adversarial reweighting）训练策略。

Result: 实验证明，该对抗性重加权方法在多种模型架构、预测任务及分布偏移场景下，均能显著改善模型在整体数据及难样本子集上的准确度与校准度权衡。

Conclusion: 本文证明了专家级校准在硬路由模型下对于整体模型的校准是充分的，但在软路由模型下则不然。通过引入对抗性重加权机制，可以有效改善分布偏移下的模型校准与准确性权衡。

Abstract: Calibration aligns a model's predictive uncertainty with the frequencies of its empirical outcomes and is important for understanding and trusting reported probabilities. Recent work shows that enforcing calibration at the level of individual predictors can improve ensemble accuracy and calibration, with mixture-of-experts (MoE) models showing strong empirical improvements in particular; however, the conditions under which calibration helps MoE are not well understood. In this work, we study how MoE models behave under distribution shift, focusing on how routing mechanisms interact with expert-level calibration. We show that expert calibration is sufficient to ensure calibration of the overall model under a broad class of distribution shifts in hard-routed models, but is insufficient for calibrating soft-routed models. To address this, we propose an adversarial reweighting that penalizes calibration errors of the routed aggregate under distribution shift, and we demonstrate that it improves the accuracy-calibration tradeoff both on average and on difficult subsets of the data, across model classes, prediction tasks, and distribution shifts.

</details>

### [130] [MonaVec: A Training-Free Embedded Vector Search Kernel for Edge and Offline AI Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19458)
*Oğuzhan Yenen*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: MonaVec 是一款面向边缘与离线环境的确定性嵌入式向量搜索内核，通过无需训练的 4-bit 量化技术和单文件存储格式，在保持极高召回率的同时，实现了类似 SQLite 的轻量级与跨平台一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的向量搜索系统通常依赖服务器架构、大容量内存或需要离线训练数据，无法满足边缘设备和离线环境下对轻量化、便携性、数据隐私以及计算确定性的严格要求。因此，作者旨在开发一种类似 SQLite 的嵌入式向量搜索内核，实现“单文件、单函数调用、随处运行”。

Method: 1. 采用 Randomized Hadamard Transform (RHDH) 进行数据无关的预处理，将输入分布转化为 N(0,1)，从而实现无需训练的 Lloyd-Max 4-bit 量化；2. 采用单文件 (.mvec) 存储架构，利用 ChaCha20 旋转种子确保跨架构的计算结果确定性；3. 使用纯 Rust 实现，支持多平台 SIMD 指令集加速，并提供 BruteForce、IvfFlat 和 HNSW 多种索引后端。

Result: 在 AG News 数据集测试中，MonaVec 4-bit BruteForce 在仅占用 27 MB 内存的情况下实现了 0.960 的 Recall@10，性能优于 float32 FAISS-IVF 和 8-bit usearch，同时确保了字节级别的计算确定性，并支持扩展至百万级向量的规模。

Conclusion: MonaVec 成功实现了在资源受限的边缘设备上进行确定性、高性能的向量搜索。它通过数据无关的量化技术和单文件存储架构，填补了嵌入式领域对于类似 SQLite 的轻量级、可移植向量检索方案的空白。

Abstract: We present MonaVec, a deterministic, embedded vector-search kernel for edge and offline AI -- settings where server infrastructure, network connectivity, and training data are all unavailable. Existing vector-search systems assume a persistent server, gigabytes of RAM, or a training pass over the corpus; MonaVec instead targets the deployment profile of SQLite: one file, one function call, runs anywhere. Its quantization core is training-free by default and data-oblivious: a Randomized Hadamard Transform (RHDH) conditions any input distribution toward N(0,1), so precomputed Lloyd-Max tables quantize to 4 bits (8x smaller) with no learned codebook and no data pass. The index persists as a single .mvec file whose embedded ChaCha20 rotation seed makes results reproducible across architectures and byte-identical within a build -- a determinism guarantee that parallel-build graph libraries cannot offer.
  On semantic embeddings (AG News, 45K x 1024-dim BGE-M3, cosine), MonaVec 4-bit BruteForce reaches 0.960 Recall@10 in 27 MB -- leading float32 FAISS-IVF and 8-bit usearch on recall -- while trading peak throughput for byte-identical determinism. A single-pass global standardization (fit()) extends the same data-oblivious pipeline to magnitude-sensitive L2 data, and optional IvfFlat and HNSW backends carry it to million-vector corpora.
  MonaVec is implemented in pure Rust with Python bindings and runtime SIMD dispatch (AVX-512/AVX2/NEON/scalar). It targets on-device RAG, offline agents, and embedded retrieval -- the niche SQLite occupies for relational data: one file, one call, runs anywhere.

</details>


### [131] [VCG: A Multimodal Retrieval Framework for E-Commerce Video Feeds under Extreme Cold-Start Conditions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19627)
*Katya Mirylenka,Egor Malykh,Mahdyar Ravanbakhsh,Michael Gygli,Marco-Andrea Buchmann,Andrew Dzhoha,Svitlana Borzenko,Francesca Catino,Mohamed Gaafar,Maarten Versteegh,Thomas Kober,Dario d'Andrea,Ellie Langhans*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文针对电商短视频流中的“极端冷启动”和交互偏差问题，提出了一种基于CLIP的多模态检索系统（VCG），通过语义映射实现了零样本内容检索，在实测中将视频深度播放完成率提升了50%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数字电商正从静态目录向沉浸式视频流转变，这导致了“极端冷启动”问题：新视频缺乏交互历史，无法使用传统的协同过滤算法。同时，沉浸式视频流中的位置和时长偏差干扰了交互信号，使得传统的推荐方法难以有效工作。因此，需要一套能够基于内容本身进行检索的系统来解决这些挑战。

Method: 该系统采用了一个基于CLIP架构的多模态检索引擎（VCG）。主要技术手段包括：1. 领域适配：对预训练的视觉-语言模型进行适配，以适应电商短视频场景；2. 语义映射：将用户偏好和视频内容映射到同一共享语义空间，从而摆脱对交互历史的依赖；3. 鉴别式模型应用：对比了生成式模型（LLM）与鉴别式模型（CLIP）的性能，并选择鉴别式模型作为核心检索基石，以避免嵌入空间塌陷。

Result: 在线A/B测试结果显示，VCG系统有效缓解了交互偏差，使得视频的深度播放完成率（Deep Video Completion）提升了50%。此外，在对比实验中发现，相较于生成式模型（LLM），基于CLIP的鉴别式模型在检索任务中表现更优，避免了嵌入空间塌陷。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了基于多模态检索的方法（VCG系统）是解决短视频电商领域冷启动问题的有效途径。研究强调了区分模型（如CLIP）在检索任务中的空间优势，并指出生成式模型（LLM）虽然具备强大的属性理解能力，但在检索任务中存在嵌入空间塌陷的问题。最终，该系统通过将视频与用户映射到共享语义空间，成功实现了零样本检索，显著提升了用户体验。

Abstract: The digital commerce landscape is shifting from static, search-driven catalogs to dynamic, immersive video feeds. This transition introduces an ``extreme cold-start'' problem: unlike traditional items, new short-form videos lack the dense interaction history required for collaborative filtering. Furthermore, immersive feeds introduce strong position and duration biases that distort standard engagement signals. In this paper, we demonstrate the Video Candidate Generation (VCG) system, a scalable multimodal retrieval engine designed to solve these challenges in a large-scale e-commerce environment. By leveraging a domain-adapted vision-language model (based on CLIP), we map users and videos into a shared semantic space, enabling zero-shot retrieval based on visual content rather than behavioral history. We detail the system's architecture and present a rigorous evaluation comparing generative (LLM) vs. discriminative (CLIP) embeddings. Our results show that while generative models excel at attribute prediction, they suffer from embedding space collapse in retrieval tasks. Online A/B testing demonstrates that VCG effectively mitigates engagement biases, yielding a 50\% uplift in deep video completion. To showcase the system's capabilities, we present an interactive demonstration featuring three bi-directional retrieval scenarios: Product-to-Video, Video-to-Product, and Zero-Shot Semantic Search.

</details>


### [132] [Token Factory: Efficiently Integrating Diverse Signals into Large Recommendation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19635)
*Xilun Chen,Shao-Chuan Wang,Baykal Cakici,Lukasz Heldt,Lichan Hong,Raghu Keshavan,Aniruddh Nath,Li Wei,Xinyang Xi*

TL;DR: 为了解决大规模推荐模型中传统特征集成带来的高计算开销和序列过长问题，本文提出了Token Factory框架，通过将特征转化为高效的“软标记”进行处理，在提升模型性能的同时显著优化了计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模推荐模型（LRMs）在处理传统推荐特征时面临挑战。现有的将信号“文本化”或创建离散表示的方法，往往会导致输入序列过长、内存占用巨大以及计算开销过高，限制了模型在工业环境中的应用效率。

Method: 提出了Token Factory框架，旨在将传统的异构推荐信号（如用户行为、物品属性等）转换为一组“软标记”（soft tokens）。这些软标记可以直接输入到基于Transformer的LRM中，从而实现对特征的高效集成与压缩，避免了将信号完全文本化带来的计算与内存压力。

Result: 实验结果表明，Token Factory能够有效集成多种异构输入特征，显著防止了提示词长度爆炸，同时在工业规模的推荐任务中提升了模型的整体预测性能。

Conclusion: Token Factory框架为在大规模推荐模型（LRM）中集成传统特征提供了一种高效且可扩展的方案。通过将异构特征压缩为软标记（soft tokens），该方法有效解决了传统方法导致的序列长度过长和计算开销过大的问题，在工业级推荐系统中具有显著的应用价值。

Abstract: Large Recommendation Models (LRMs) have demonstrated promising capabilities in industry-scale recommendation tasks. However, holistically integrating traditional signals into these transformer-based architectures effectively and efficiently remains a major challenge. Conventional approaches that "textualize" these signals directly or create discrete item representations often lead to excessively long prompts, substantial memory footprints, and high computational overhead. To overcome these limitations, we propose "Token Factory", a framework designed to transform traditional signals into "soft tokens" that can be directly processed by LRMs. This approach enables efficient integration and compression of heterogeneous input features, preventing prompt length explosion while enhancing model performance. We detail the architecture of Token Factory and present experimental results validating its effectiveness in a production-scale recommendation environment.

### [133] [SAFE-Cascade: Cost-Adaptive Vision-Language Routing for Chart Question Answering](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19646)
*Ayush Dwivedi,Qixin Wang,Ashvi Soni,Ruoteng Wang,Han Li,Animesh Mahapatra,Neeraj Agrawal,Xintao Wu*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: SAFE-Cascade 是一款成本自适应的图表问答系统，通过智能路由决定是否调用昂贵的 VLM，在保持高准确率的同时显著降低了推理成本和延迟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前的视觉语言模型在处理图表问答时计算成本高昂，但许多简单问题仅需 OCR 提取的文本和轻量级语言推理即可解决，因此需要一种成本自适应的方案来按需调用模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SAFE-Cascade 的交互式系统，包含三个关键步骤：1. 使用 OCR 提取图表文本信息；2. 利用轻量级文本语言模型获取初步答案；3. 通过一个基于随机森林（Random Forest）的路由学习器，评估是否需要调用 VLM。用户可以动态调整升级阈值来平衡准确性与成本。

Result: 在 ChartQA 数据集测试中，SAFE-Cascade 在保持与全 VLM 基准相当的准确率（69.1% 对 67.7%）的同时，减少了 26.9% 的 VLM 调用频率，并降低了 9.3% 的预估成本。

Conclusion: SAFE-Cascade 通过选择性模态路由机制，证明了在图表问答任务中，无需对所有查询都依赖昂贵的视觉语言模型（VLM）。该系统实现了性能与成本的有效平衡，不仅降低了计算开销，还通过可视化决策过程显著提升了系统的透明度与可解释性。

Abstract: Vision-language models (VLMs) are powerful for chart question answering, but invoking a VLM for every query can be unnecessarily expensive when many questions are answerable from OCR text and lightweight language reasoning. We demonstrate SAFE-Cascade, an interactive system for cost-adaptive chart question answering. Given a chart image and a natural-language question, SAFE-Cascade first extracts chart text with OCR, obtains a provisional answer from a text-only language model, and then uses a learned router to decide whether to accept the text answer or escalate to a VLM. The demo exposes this decision process to users: OCR evidence, text-only answer, routing probability, escalation decision, final answer, estimated cost, and estimated latency are shown side by side. SAFE-Cascade is designed as a transparent interface for understanding when visual grounding is actually needed. Users can upload or select charts, ask questions, inspect the evidence used by each pathway, compare text-only and VLM answers, and adjust the escalation threshold to explore the accuracy-cost frontier. The system is implemented with Azure Document Intelligence for OCR, gpt-5-mini as the text-only model, gemini-2.5-flash-image as the VLM, and a Random Forest router trained on inference-time features. On a held-out ChartQA test split of 375 examples from a 2,500-example experiment, SAFE-Cascade achieves 69.1% unified accuracy with 73.1% VLM invocation, compared with 67.7% accuracy and 100% VLM invocation for the full-VLM baseline. The observed +1.4 percentage-point difference is statistically uncertain, so we interpret SAFE-Cascade as matching full-VLM performance while reducing VLM calls by 26.9% and estimated cost by 9.3%. The demonstration shows how selective modality routing can make multimodal knowledge systems more transparent, tunable, and cost-aware.

</details>


### [134] [Closing the Calibration Gap in Semantic Caching](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19719)
*Aditeya Baral,Radoslav Ralev,Iliya Sotirov Zhechev,Srijith Rajamohan,Jen Agarwal*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 本文揭示了语义缓存评估中传统排序指标（PR-AUC）的局限性，提出了更符合实际部署需求的评估指标，并指出提升缓存系统性能的关键在于优化模型的校准能力而非仅仅关注排序质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 指出传统的 PR-AUC 指标无法衡量缓存系统在固定阈值下的可用性，导致模型选择与实际部署效果脱节（即高 PR-AUC 的模型在实际运行中表现往往最差）。

Method: 提出了两种新型评估指标：P-CHR AUC（衡量缓存利用水平下的精度）和 CRR（衡量离线排序质量在部署时的保持程度）；并提出了一个框架，将离线与部署间的性能差距分解为可恢复的校准组件和不可约的结构组件。

Result: 实验表明，部署质量差距主要由训练目标决定而非数据规模，且事后校准（Post-hoc calibration）只能部分弥补该差距。

Conclusion: 语义缓存的模型选择本质上是一个校准问题，而非单纯的排序问题。研究强调了在评估中引入缓存感知指标（如 P-CHR AUC）对于缩小离线评估与在线部署性能差距的关键性。

Abstract: Semantic caching cuts LLM inference costs by serving a cached response to semantically similar queries. Standard practice evaluates these systems using PR-AUC, a metric that only measures how well scores rank and ignores whether they are usable at a fixed threshold. We show this mismatch leads to systematically poor deployment choices, as models with the highest PR-AUC are often the worst in operation. We introduce Precision-Cache Hit Ratio (P-CHR) AUC, a cache-aware metric that measures precision across cache utilization levels, and Calibration Retention Rate (CRR), which captures how much offline ranking quality survives at deployment. We decompose the operational gap between offline and deployed quality into a recoverable calibration component and an irreducible structural component fixed by the dataset's positive rate. Our experiments show that the calibration gap is governed by the training objective rather than data scale, and post-hoc calibration only partially closes it. Ultimately, model selection for semantic caching is a calibration problem, not a ranking one, and measuring it is the first step to closing the gap.

</details>


### [135] [Stellar: Scalable Multimodal Document Retrieval for Natural Language Queries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19960)
*Yuxiang Guo,Zhonghao Hu,Yuren Mao,Yuhang Liu,Congcong Ge,Xiaolu Zhang,Jun Zhou,Yunjun Gao*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: Stellar是一个高效的多模态文档检索框架，通过词法过滤与磁盘驱动的延迟交互技术，解决了多向量表示带来的内存瓶颈，大幅提升了检索系统的扩展性与部署可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多模态文档检索方法（如多向量表示与延迟交互技术）虽有效，但由于产生大量的token级嵌入，导致内存开销巨大、扩展性差，难以在真实大规模场景中部署。

Method: 1. 基于词法表示的过滤（LRF）：利用微调后的多模态大模型（MLLM）作为稀疏编码器生成词法表示，实现高效候选集筛选；2. 高效磁盘驱动延迟交互（DLI）：设计了基于平衡聚类算法的磁盘存储布局，并引入代价模型，仅在运行时将必要的标记（token）嵌入加载至内存。

Result: 在四个基准测试及一个大规模数据集上的实验表明，Stellar在不降低检索效果的前提下，将内存开销和查询延迟降低了1至2个数量级。

Conclusion: Stellar框架通过结合词法过滤与磁盘驱动的延迟交互机制，成功克服了多模态文档检索中多向量表示带来的高内存开销问题，为大规模RAG系统提供了兼顾性能与效率的现实可行方案。

Abstract: Multimodal document retrieval--selecting the most relevant multimodal document from a large corpus to answer a natural language query--plays an essential role in Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems. State-of-the-art methods represent each document and query with multiple token-level embeddings and use late interaction to achieve high effectiveness. However, such multi-vector representations incur substantial memory overhead during retrieval, leading to poor scalability and hindering real-world deployment. In this paper, we present Stellar, a scalable multimodal document retrieval framework that stores token-level document embeddings on disk and loads only a small set of candidate embeddings into memory for late interaction. Stellar comprises two key components: (i) Lexical Representation-based Filtering (LRF), which fine-tunes a Multimodal Large Language Model (MLLM) as a sparse encoder to produce high-quality lexical representations, enabling efficient and effective document filtering to significantly reduce the candidate set; (ii) Efficient Disk-backed Late Interaction (DLI), which designs an on-disk token embedding storage layout guided by a balanced clustering algorithm, and dynamically loads only the necessary token embeddings into memory using a simple yet effective cost model. Extensive experiments on four real-world benchmarks and a newly presented large-scale dataset demonstrate that Stellar reduces memory overhead and query latency by 1-2 orders of magnitude compared to existing methods without compromising retrieval effectiveness.

</details>


### [136] [PACMS: Submodular Context Selection as a Pluggable Engine for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20047)
*Manu Ghulyani,Arunabh Singh,Karan Bharadwaj,Ankit Nath,Suranjan Goswami*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 大语言模型代理目前的上下文窗口管理（如最近截断法）因忽视信息相关性而导致重要记忆丢失。本文主张建立一种统一的、基于相关性的上下文管理机制，以便在有限的 token 预算内动态留存最关键的对话历史、内存信息和工具反馈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在长期对话和工具使用过程中，上下文窗口会被快速填满。传统的“最近截断”（recency truncation）策略不仅缺乏对主题的理解，容易导致关键但较早的信息被丢失，且无法有效处理冗长但无关的工具输出，从而限制了代理在长跨度任务中的记忆和推理能力。

Method: 本文指出当前的大模型上下文管理存在缺陷，并提出了一个构想方向：将对话轮次、持久化内存和工具输出视为一个统一的候选池，通过基于相关性的动态选择机制（而非简单的基于时间的截断）来优化上下文窗口的利用率。

Result: 分析表明，现有的RAG（检索增强生成）和上下文压缩方法在处理代理当前的上下文池时存在局限性，无法根据当前任务需求智能地仲裁和筛选已有的上下文信息。这些方法往往是“查询盲”或“全局盲”的，不能解决长期记忆与上下文容量限制之间的矛盾。

Conclusion: 现有的基于时间顺序的上下文截断机制无法满足长期对话中对特定信息的需求。研究者建议将对话历史、持久化内存和工具输出整合为统一的候选池，并根据当前查询的相关性进行动态选择和管理，而非仅依赖简单的截断策略。

Abstract: Conversational and tool-using LLM agents operate over a context window that fills from several directions simultaneously. As a session proceeds, the agent accumulates user and assistant turns, entries drawn from a persistent memory store, and often largest of all, the verbatim outputs of tool calls such as file reads, search results, and API responses. Once the cumulative context exceeds the model's token budget, the framework must decide what to keep.
  The prevailing mechanism is recency truncation, sometimes paired with periodic summarization. This is topic-blind: a fact established early in a session is discarded simply because it is old, even when the current user query is about exactly that fact; conversely, verbose but irrelevant recent material is retained. Agents that must recall information across many turns, the defining case for memory, are precisely where recency truncation fails.
  Existing alternatives sit outside the agent's assembly step. Retrieval augmented generation fetches external documents into the prompt but does not arbitrate the agent's \emph{already-present} pooled context. Context-compression methods reduce token count by rewriting or pruning text, but operate query-blind and lossily. Neither treats memory entries, conversation turns, and tool outputs as a single candidate pool to be selected from by relevance at the moment the prompt is assembled.

</details>


### [137] [Generative Engine Optimization at Scale: Measuring Brand Visibility Across AI Search Engines](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20065)
*Pratyush Kumar*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 随着AI搜索取代传统搜索，品牌需要转向“生成式引擎优化（GEO）”。本研究分析了10万条AI响应，揭示了品牌规模对AI可见度的决定性影响，指出企业官网和列表式内容是获取引用的关键，并提出了优化AI品牌曝光的初步策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着用户转向ChatGPT、Perplexity等AI搜索引擎获取答案，传统的SEO已无法满足需求。研究旨在探讨品牌如何应对这一转型，即如何测量和提升品牌在AI生成引擎中的可见度（GEO/AEO），特别是对于非头部品牌（如中小企业和初创公司）的挑战。

Method: 研究团队分析了2026年3月至5月期间，基于Ranqo平台追踪的100多个品牌的10万多条提示响应数据，评估了品牌在AI搜索中的可见度、引用来源偏好、内容类型及情感倾向，并以此构建基准。

Result: 研究发现品牌可见度呈现明显的“三级阶梯”：顶级品牌出现率为73%，中型品牌为44%，小型品牌仅为11%；AI引擎倾向于引用企业官网，其次是YouTube和Reddit；“最佳/推荐”列表类文章是最高效的内容形式；品牌情感倾向相比于品牌提及率更容易发生波动。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了生成式引擎优化（GEO）的初步基准，证明了AI品牌可见度是可以量化的，且受品牌成熟度影响巨大。研究提出的七项初步协议为未来改善品牌AI可见度提供了实践方向。

Abstract: People increasingly get answers straight from AI search engines like ChatGPT, Claude, Perplexity, and Gemini rather than scrolling search results. Brands that once focused on search engine optimization (SEO) must now optimize for how these engines represent, cite, and recommend them -- a shift variously called Generative Engine Optimization (GEO), Answer Engine Optimization (AEO), and AI Search Visibility. We treat AEO and AI Visibility as part of GEO, and study how to measure brand visibility across AI engines: what they value when they cite a brand, which sources they rely on, and what content large language models surface. The hard case is everyone outside the already-authoritative top brands -- SMEs, D2C brands, creators, and early-stage startups.
  We analyze 100K+ prompt responses across 100+ brands tracked on Ranqo between March and May 2026. First visibility runs form a clear three-tier brand-stature ladder: global household names (e.g., Stripe, Nike) appear in 73% of relevant AI answers on their first run; established mid-market and regional brands (e.g., Olipop, Klaviyo) in 44%; niche and small brands in just 11% -- about 30 percentage points per step. When engines cite sources, about 78% go to corporate websites; among non-corporate sources YouTube leads, ahead of Reddit, editorial media, and Wikipedia. The highest-leverage page is the ranked "best-of" listicle, the most-cited content format at about 21% of all citations. Sentiment is the unstable signal: whether a brand is framed positively or negatively flips about 6.7 times more often than whether it is mentioned at all.
  These findings provide a first large-scale baseline for measuring GEO: AI brand visibility can be measured, differs by platform, and varies strongly by brand maturity. We close by proposing seven v1.1 protocols to test whether specific recommendations can causally improve AI visibility.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建了一个包含 1000 多个计算机科学主题和四种代表性研究意图（方法导向、设置锚定、基于比较、范围受控）的大规模分类基准数据集 ScholarQuest，并配套提供共享检索后端 ScholarBase 以确保评估的可重复性。

Abstract: Academic paper search is a core step in scientific research, and LLM-based search agents are emerging as a promising paradigm for iterative, intent-driven literature exploration. However, existing benchmarks are insufficient for systematically evaluating agentic academic search under realistic open literature environments. We propose ScholarQuest, a large-scale, taxonomy-guided benchmark for agentic academic paper search. ScholarQuest is constructed from over 1,000 computer science topics and four representative research intents, including method-oriented, setting-anchored, comparison-based, and scope-controlled queries. It further provides scalable answer construction and a shared retrieval backend ScholarBase for reproducible evaluation. Benchmarking results show that agentic methods outperform single-shot retrieval baselines, yet the best-performing agent only achieves 0.314 Recall@100 and 0.355 Recall@All, indicating substantial room for improvement. In addition, analyses of search efficiency, intent-level robustness, and failure cases further highlight the benchmark's ability to provide multi-dimensional evaluation signals for academic paper search agents.

### [139] [ELVA: Exploring Ranking-Driven Universal Multimodal Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20280)
*Yuhan Liu,Pei Fu,Hang Li,Yukun Qi,Chao Jiang,Jingwen Fu,Zhen Liu,Bin Qin,Zhenbo Luo,Jian Luan,Jingmin Xin*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对多模态大模型在检索任务中忽略查询细粒度信息（粒度盲点）的问题，论文提出了ELVA框架。该框架通过基于规则的强化学习和细粒度负样本处理策略，提升了模型对复杂查询的理解力，并在自建基准MRBench上取得了显著的效果提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在通用多模态检索任务中，现有的基于对比学习的MLLM范式存在“粒度盲点”问题。由于对比学习仅将样本简单分类为正负，导致模型忽略了查询中关键的细粒度信息，无法有效处理复杂的检索任务。因此，需要一种能够利用负样本中的差异化信息来提升模型对细粒度特征感知能力的方法。

Method: 1. 提出ELVA框架：通过基于规则的强化学习（RLVR）优化模型，无需显式的排名标签，使模型能够探索新的排名行为。
2. 细粒度负样本处理：摒弃了传统的二元分类对比学习，根据负样本与正样本的相似度进行差异化处理，从而学习不同的粒度信息。
3. 引入MRBench基准：开发了一个专门用于评估多粒度查询场景的基准测试，以更精确地衡量模型的“粒度盲点”。

Result: 1. ELVA在多个标准检索基准测试中均达到了SOTA（最先进）性能。
2. 在专门针对多粒度查询设计的MRBench测试中，ELVA取得了13.1%的显著性能提升，证明了该方法在缓解粒度盲点方面的有效性。

Conclusion: ELVA 通过引入基于规则的强化学习框架，成功解决了通用多模态检索（UMR）中存在的“粒度盲点”问题。该研究证明了利用细粒度负样本进行差异化处理以及在缺乏明确标签的情况下通过可验证奖励进行模型优化，是提升复杂多模态检索性能的有效途径。同时，提出的MRBench基准为评估模型对多粒度查询的理解能力提供了有力支持。

Abstract: Leveraging Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) via contrastive learning has become a mainstream paradigm for improving the performance of Universal Multimodal Retrieval (UMR). However, previous works have ignored the grain blindness when adapting the contrastive paradigm into retrieval tasks. Grain blindness refers to the tendency of the model to overlook grain-level information contained in the query, which is crucial for effectively handling complex queries. This stems from contrastive learning treating samples as a binary classification (positive/negative), while ignoring the different information carried by each negative sample. To address this, we argue that negatives should be treated differently according to their similarity to the positive sample, enabling the model to learn distinct grain information from each negative. In this paper, we introduce a simple but effective framework, called ELVA, a novel rule-based RL framework that mitigates grain blindness through ranking-driven MLLMs. 1) Instead of relying on reward models, we extend Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards
  (RLVR) to retrieval tasks, allowing the model to explore new ranking behaviors without explicit ranking labels. 2) By utilizing rule-based rewards, our approach jointly optimizes the ranking of negative samples while enlarging the similarity gap between positive and negative. To more precisely measure grain blindness, we further introduce MRBench, a new benchmark specifically designed for multi-grain query scenarios. ELVA achieves state-of-the-art results across standard retrieval benchmarks, and its notable 13.1% improvement on MRBench further demonstrates its effectiveness in alleviating grain blindness.

</details>


### [140] [Structuring and Tokenizing Distributed User Interest Context for Generative Recommendation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.20554)
*Ruizhong Qiu,Yinglong Xia,Dongqi Fu,Hanqing Zeng,Ren Chen,Xiangjun Fan,Hong Li,Hong Yan,Hanghang Tong*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: 针对生成式推荐中上下文建模不足的问题，G2Rec 提出了一种统一的图结构与语义标记框架，实现了在大规模工业场景下对用户兴趣的高效、精准捕捉，且无需标注数据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有生成式推荐模型在处理物品标记（item tokenization）时存在局限：基于图的方法难以兼顾可扩展性与全局信息；基于启发式的语义标记方法则缺乏有效的监督信号，导致语义表示不够精确，无法有效捕捉复杂的上下文信息。

Method: 提出名为 G2Rec 的框架，将全局图结构的协同交互建模与语义标记技术进行统一。该方法通过整合复杂的用户行为上下文与物品语义信息，无需显式标注的用户兴趣数据，即可实现对用户兴趣原型的捕捉。

Result: 在公开数据集上的广泛实验表明，G2Rec 在性能上优于现有的基准方法。此外，该模型已成功部署于工业级产品场景中，验证了其在实际大规模生产环境下的有效性与稳健性。

Conclusion: G2Rec 通过统一全局图结构建模与语义标记，不仅规避了传统方法在扩展性与语义表达上的缺陷，还通过无监督的方式捕捉到更全面、准确的用户兴趣原型，为工业界生成式推荐系统提供了一种高效且可扩展的解决方案。

Abstract: Generative recommendation is an emerging paradigm that has shown promise in industrial recommendation systems, aiming to predict users' next interactions from their historical behaviors. At the core of generative recommendation lies item tokenization, which bridges item semantics and recommendation models. However, existing methods often struggle to effectively organize and inject complex user-behavioral and item-semantic contexts into recommendation models simultaneously. On the one hand, existing graph-based integration methods, such as graph serialization and graph neural networks, either suffer from scalability issues or exploit only local graph information. On the other hand, existing semantic tokenization methods typically rely on heuristics and lack explicit supervision signals, which may lead to inaccurate or suboptimal semantic representations. To address these limitations in user interest context modeling, we propose G2Rec, a scalable framework that unifies holistic graph-based user co-engagement modeling with semantic tokenization for industrial-scale generative recommendation. Overall, G2Rec enables recommendation models to capture holistic and semantically grounded user interest prototypes without requiring ground-truth user interests, thereby providing more comprehensive and accurate modeling of user behavior contexts in industrial sequential recommendation. Online deployment across product surfaces and extensive experiments on public datasets demonstrate the superiority of G2Rec over existing methods.

</details>

### [141] [Computational Identifiability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19361)
*Lucius E. J. Bynum,Rajesh Ranganath,Kyunghyun Cho*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文引入“计算可识别性”框架，通过有限计算搜索过程替代传统理想化假设，实现了在有限数据和复杂因果场景下对因果效应的实用化识别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的因果识别理论多基于大样本、渐近性或数学理想化假设，难以解决现实世界中存在的小样本、数据缺失或因果图模糊等实际限制，因此作者旨在建立一种更具实践导向、受计算能力限制的识别框架。

Method: 作者提出了“计算可识别性”框架，核心在于将识别问题转化为一个有限计算搜索过程。该过程基于对参数的先验分布及特定的搜索算法，在指定的误差容忍度内寻找经验估计量，从而判断目标因果量是否可识别。

Result: 通过多项实验验证，该框架成功解决了多种复杂场景下的识别问题，包括有限小样本分析、模糊因果图标准下的识别、观测与干预数据的混合处理，以及复杂反事实估计量的计算识别。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了一种名为“计算可识别性”（computational identifiability）的新范式，通过有限计算搜索过程取代了传统的理论化假设，为因果推理提供了更具现实意义和应用价值的识别评估框架，特别是在处理小样本、模糊图形标准及复杂数据类型时表现出显著优势。

Abstract: Identification conditions describe the computability of a target query or parameter of interest as a function of the type and amount of information available. In causal identification, this information is often expressed in the form of a causal graph, and data are observed or collected for some subset of variables in the graph. Target queries may be for a single effect alone or for a class of effects in a given model. The derivation of an identification algorithm then defines mathematically the process by which the desired causal effect(s) can be uniquely determined, theoretically, in expectation. Identifiability in expectation, or 'theoretical identifiability,' generally assumes asymptotic properties, infinite data, or other mathematically idealized conditions. In this paper, we explore a fundamental distinction between this theoretical, idealized notion of identifiability and a proposed alternative that is computation-bound. The framework we propose - 'computational identifiability' - is to instead define a finite computational search procedure for an empirical estimator. If this process finds an estimator empirically, within a desired error tolerance, then identifiability is satisfied, conditional on the specified assumptions of the search (i.e., a prior distribution over the parameters) and conditional on the search procedure itself. Through several experiments, we demonstrate how this framework allows us to answer fine-grained, practical identification questions, such as identification with small finite samples, with ambiguous graphical criteria, with mixed observational-interventional data, and across counterfactual data and estimands. Code is available at https://github.com/lbynum/metadentify.

</details>


### [142] [When to Trust, How to Distill: Multi-Foundation Model Guidance for Lightweight, Robust Scientific Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19363)
*Rupasree Dey,Abdul Matin,Nathan Orwick,Yao Zhang,Shrideep Pallickara,Sangmi Lee Pallickara*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 为解决时间序列基础模型在科学领域应用时的“分布偏移”与“计算成本过高”难题，该论文提出了Guard框架。通过动态路由机制和不确定性门控蒸馏，该方法能从多个不完美的教师模型中高效提取知识，训练出轻量级且高精度的科学领域专用预测器，适用于边缘计算场景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间序列基础模型（TSFM）在科学领域应用时面临两个核心痛点：一是分布偏移导致的零样本性能不佳，二是计算量巨大，难以在边缘计算传感器网络中部署。本研究旨在探索如何从这些分布失准的基础模型中提取潜在的结构化知识，以训练轻量化的专业预测模型。

Method: 提出了一种名为Guard（Gated Uncertainty-Aware Routing for Distillation）的新框架，包含两个核心机制：1. 上下文路由（Contextual Router）：基于输入数据的局部统计特征，动态选择最相关的教师模型；2. 不确定性门控温度机制（Uncertainty-Gated Temperature）：当教师模型预测置信度与领域现实不符时，自动调节知识蒸馏的强度，防止负迁移。

Result: 在气象、生态碳通量、土壤湿度和能源电网等四个气候关键领域进行了评估。结果表明，Guard相比于固定权重的多教师蒸馏基线显著降低了RMSE。即便在原始教师模型零样本准确率不佳的情况下，Guard仍能提取到有效信息，并在28.5%的复杂案例中超越了全局表现最优的基础模型。

Conclusion: Guard框架有效解决了基础模型在特定科学领域中的分布偏移问题，证明了通过动态路由和不确定性感知机制，可以从“零样本”表现欠佳的多个教师模型中提取关键知识，从而实现在资源受限边缘设备上的高精度科学预测。

Abstract: The deployment of Time-Series Foundation Models (TSFMs) in physical sciences is hindered by a critical trade-off: while these models encode rich, universal temporal dynamics, they suffer from severe distributional misalignment when applied zero-shot to specific scientific domains, and their computational cost prohibits deployment in edge-computing sensor networks. We address a fundamental challenge: How can we extract latent structural knowledge from misaligned foundation models (FM) to train lightweight, specialized forecasters? We propose Gated Uncertainty-Aware Routing for Distillation (Guard), a novel framework that reframes multiteacher distillation as an instance-wise decision process with two adaptive mechanisms: (1) a Contextual Router that dynamically selects the most relevant teacher based on local input statistics, exploiting complementarity across diverse foundation models; and (2) an Uncertainty-Gated Temperature mechanism that acts as a "circuit-breaker," automatically attenuating distillation strength when teacher confidence diverges from domain reality. We evaluate our proposed lightweight framework on four climate-critical domains: meteorology, ecosystem carbon flux, soil moisture, and energy grids. Our method significantly reduces RMSE relative to a fixed-weight multi-teacher distillation baseline, successfully distilling knowledge from pretrained FMs (teachers) even when they exhibit suboptimal zero-shot accuracy due to distribution shift between the original and target data domains. We demonstrate that these domain-misaligned teachers can still serve as critical correctives, outperforming the globally superior FMs on 28.5% of the hardest instances. Ultimately, this enables high-precision scientific forecasting suitable for resource-constrained edge deployment. Code is available at https://github.com/RupasreeDey/GUARD-KDD2026.

### [143] [Closing the Social-Semantic Gap: SPSD for Edge-Based Prompt Compression in Cloud LLM Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19364)
*Abhinit Sen,Ajeet Kumar,Manaranjan Pradhan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SPSD通过在边缘侧利用小型模型压缩用户提示词中的社交冗余信息，在几乎不损失模型响应质量的情况下，显著降低了云端大模型的输入成本与能源消耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大模型推理阶段的预填充（Prefill）过程消耗了大量的云端计算资源。人类日常交流中存在大量非推理必需的“社交脚手架”式冗余文本（即所谓的“社会-语义鸿沟”），这些文本增加了输入Token的数量，从而推高了计算成本和能源消耗。

Method: 提出了一种名为SPSD（情感保留语义蒸馏）的边缘侧管线。该方法利用4位量化的小型语言模型（SLM，如Gemma-2-2B-Instruct）在用户端对提示词进行压缩，去除其中包含“社交脚手架”（如客套话、冗余表述）但语义信息量较低的内容，仅将压缩后的关键语义传输至云端大模型（如Llama-3.1-8B）。同时，针对安全关键领域，引入了基于规则的门控机制以确保直接传输。

Result: 在248个提示词的测试集上，SPSD平均每次调用节省约99.9个输入Token。在盲测评估中，蒸馏后的提示词与原始提示词在响应质量上表现出非劣效性（43%持平，28%蒸馏胜出，29%原始胜出）。估计每次调用的净能源节省约为70-270微瓦时（uWh）。

Conclusion: SPSD证明，通过端侧小型语言模型对用户提示词进行语义压缩，可以在保证大模型推理质量的前提下，显著降低云端大模型的输入Token开销及能源消耗，为边缘计算与云端模型的高效协同提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The prefill stage of Large Language Model (LLM) inference is a growing contributor to cloud-scale energy cost. Many consumer-support and conversational prompts contain social scaffolding: politeness markers, apologetic preamble, repetition, and rapport-building language that is important for human communication but carries low marginal information for machine reasoning. We call this discrepancy the Social-Semantic Gap. We present SPSD (Sentiment Preserving Semantic Distillation), an edge-based pipeline that compresses user prompts using a 4-bit quantised Small Language Model before transmission to a cloud-deployed LLM. Evaluation on a 248-prompt corpus using Gemma-2-2B-Instruct (Q4_K_M) as the SLM and Llama-3.1-8B-Instruct as the cloud evaluation model yields a mean input token saving of 99.9 tokens per distilled call, with all 146 distilled calls yielding positive savings. Response quality, assessed by blind LLM-as-judge scoring across 121 pairs, is non-inferior to the raw path within a pre-specified 1-point margin on a 15-point rubric; the judge awarded 43 percent ties, 28 percent distilled wins, and 29 percent raw wins. Cosine similarity is mixed: mean 0.682, median 0.712, with 54.1 percent of pairs above the 0.70 reference threshold. Safety-critical domains are conservatively routed to passthrough via rule-based gates. Per-call net energy saving is estimated at 70-270 uWh under stated assumptions. SPSD shows that on-device prompt distillation can reduce cloud LLM input-token cost while preserving response quality within a practical non-inferiority margin.

Abstract: Diffusion models have become essential for high-fidelity 3D MRI synthesis, yet their deployment remains constrained by substantial GPU resource demands arising from hundreds of U-Net evaluations per sample and a highly heterogeneous kernel behavior. This paper performs a comprehensive performance analysis of the state-of-the-art medical diffusion model, Med-DDPM, across three generations of NVIDIA architectures to study kernel-level runtime breakdowns, instruction-mix characteristics, memory system utilization, warp-level activities, and profiler priority-score estimates. We show that training is overwhelmingly dominated by cuDNN convolution and implicit-GEMM kernels, with inefficiencies arising from memory-access patterns, tensor-layout conversions, and limited Tensor Core utilization. Guided by these insights, we evaluate two architecture-aware optimizations TF32 Tensor Core activation and a 3D channels-last layout and demonstrate that they reduce SM cycles by up to 100x, cut dynamic instructions by 100x, raise Tensor Core utilization from 1.45 to 9.98x, and increase IPC by 7% on A100, all without degrading synthesis quality.

### [145] [Information Lattice Learning as Probabilistic Graphical Model Structure Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19366)
*Haizi Yu,Lav R. Varshney*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该文通过将信息格学习（ILL）与概率图模型（PGM）相结合，证明了ILL学习到的规则等价于对商变量施加的边缘约束，从而将其确立为一种新型的可解释因子图结构学习方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在解决如何从信号中学习可解释规则的问题，并试图构建一种桥梁，将信息格学习（ILL）这一抽象的代数学习方法与经典的概率图模型（PGM）理论联系起来，以提升模型的可解释性和数学严谨性。

Method: 提出了一种基于信息格（Information Lattice）的学习框架，通过在表征抽象层级的划分格上交替进行投影（学习规则）与提升（还原信号）操作。对于概率质量函数，ILL利用L2一致性原则（类似于最大熵）进行分布重建，并推导了其与对数线性因子图的数学联系。

Result: 证明了ILL学习到的概率规则可以自然地解释为概率图模型中的边缘约束；揭示了在香农熵约束下，ILL生成的提升分布等价于一种由学习到的抽象所索引的对数线性因子图。

Conclusion: 信息格学习（ILL）本质上是关于商变量的、可解释的约束型因子图的结构学习方法。该视角明确了ILL与图模型及最大熵模型的关系，并为推理、可识别性及符号-概率混合学习提供了新的研究方向。

Abstract: Information lattice learning (ILL) learns interpretable rules of a signal by alternately projecting the signal onto a partition lattice that encodes a hierarchy of abstractions and lifting selected rules back to the signal domain. When the signal is a probability mass function, we show the probabilistic rules learned by ILL admit a natural probabilistic graphical model (PGM) interpretation and develop this interpretation in detail. A partition in ILL induces a deterministic quotient variable, and a rule is the marginal law of that quotient variable. A rule set is therefore a collection of marginal constraints over interpretable abstractions. General lifting is the feasible family of all joint distributions satisfying those constraints, while special lifting chooses a maximum-ignorance reconstruction, implemented in ILL by an L2 uniformity principle closely related to maximum entropy. Under a Shannon-entropy lifting, the same constraints yield a log-linear factor graph whose factors are indexed by learned abstractions. The information lattice itself, however, is not a Bayesian network: its edges encode refinement and coarsening of abstractions, not conditional dependence. Thus ILL is best viewed as structure learning for interpretable constraint-based factor graphs over quotient variables. This view clarifies how ILL relates to graphical models and maximum entropy models, while suggesting new directions for inference, identifiability, and hybrid symbolic-probabilistic learning.

### [146] [Weibull Weight-Scale Parameter Evolution under AdamW Training Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19367)
*Tiexin Ding*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过“三力分解”模型解释了AdamW训练中Transformer权重分布参数λ的演变过程，发现对齐力主导了权重尺度的增长，并提出了一种从稀疏检查点准确恢复训练动态的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在阐明Transformer模型在AdamW训练过程中，权重分布的Weibull尺度参数λ表现出的增长、过冲及随后松弛这一非单调动态行为背后的驱动机制。

Method: 研究基于两参数Weibull分布框架，推导了AdamW更新过程中权重平方范数的“三力分解”模型（对齐力、注入力、衰减力）。利用Pythia-70M模型进行实证分析，并引入样条位移法（spline displacement method）从稀疏检查点中恢复对齐力，以克服缺少优化器矩信息的限制。

Result: 研究发现，在训练初期，对齐力是主导因素（贡献88-94%的力预算）；在饱和阶段，对齐力与衰减力达到平衡，导致权重尺度从增长转为松弛。此外，样条位移法在恢复对齐力方面表现出92-94%的准确率，且实验发现λ的峰值受训练数据一致性影响。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了AdamW训练过程中Transformer权重分布Weibull分布尺度参数λ动态演化的物理机制，通过三力分解模型解释了其增长、过冲与松弛现象，并提出了一种基于样条位移的评估方法，为理解深度学习优化动态提供了新的理论视角。

Abstract: Building on a two-parameter Weibull framework for diagnosing transformer weight distributions, we study why the Weibull weight-scale parameter $λ$ grows, overshoots, and then relaxes during AdamW training. We derive a leading-order three-force decomposition of the squared weight norm from the AdamW update: an alignment force measuring the correlation between weights and the adaptive update direction, an injection force from adaptive step magnitude, and a decay force from decoupled weight decay. On self-trained Pythia-70M models with ground-truth optimizer moments, alignment dominates the rise phase, contributing 88-94% of the absolute force budget across four random seeds and remaining robust to super-weight removal. Near saturation, alignment and decay approach balance, explaining the transition from weight-scale growth to relaxation. These force dynamics directly govern the squared-norm component underlying $λ(t)$; the remaining RMS-to-Weibull reconstruction offset is measurable and decomposes into bridge and integration components, totaling approximately 5-6% in densely sampled regions. To extend the analysis to real models where optimizer moments are unavailable, we introduce a spline displacement method that recovers the alignment force from sparse checkpoints with approximately 92-94% accuracy, about twice the naive two-point baseline. We further observe that the peak value of $λ(t)$ varies with training-data coherence in our experiments, suggesting a data-dependent component of weight-scale growth that we leave to a controlled follow-up study. Code and data are available at https://github.com/tiexinding/NPM-Weibull-public.

### [147] [Zero-Inflated Gaussian Distributions Enable Parameter-Space Sparsity in Estimation-of-Distribution Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19369)
*Andreas Faust,Sven Nitzsche,Juergen Becker*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文通过引入零膨胀高斯模型（ZIG），将分布估计算法扩展至稀疏优化领域，实现了稀疏模式与参数值的自动联合优化，避免了人工算子设计并提升了复杂任务下的黑盒优化效率。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的演化算法在处理稀疏黑盒优化问题时，往往需要依赖人工设计的稀疏算子、阈值处理等偏差方案，违背了分布估计算法（EDA）避免人工干预的设计初衷。现有技术缺乏一种能够通用且高效地处理稀疏参数空间的分布模型。

Method: 提出了基于零膨胀高斯（ZIG）分布的分布估计算法。通过引入包含指示变量（代表稀疏模式）和值变量（代表参数取值）的潜高斯模型，实现对参数及其相关性的联合建模，并采用摊销逆（amortized inversion）技术进行参数估计。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于零膨胀高斯（ZIG）分布的分布估计算法（EDA）有效地弥补了传统EDA在稀疏优化领域的缺失。该方法通过联合建模稀疏模式和活动参数，实现了无需手动设计算子的稀疏黑盒优化，证明了在复杂任务中具有优越的收敛速度和性能。

Abstract: Estimation-of-distribution algorithms (EDAs) are a powerful class of evolutionary methods for black-box optimization, especially when little is known about the structure of the objective. Whereas classical evolutionary algorithms rely on hand-designed mutation and crossover operators, hard to devise for unknown problem structures, and a source of bias, EDAs sidestep operator design entirely: they fit a probability distribution to the best individuals and sample the next generation from it. EDAs are well established on continuous parameter spaces, but they have not previously been generalized to sparse ones, in which most coefficients of a good solution are exactly zero. Existing sparse black-box optimizers therefore reintroduce exactly what EDAs were designed to avoid: hand-crafted sparsity operators, bi-level schemes alternating between support set and active values, zeroing thresholds, and other baked-in assumptions. We close this gap by proposing multivariate zero-inflated Gaussian (ZIG) distributions as EDA sampling laws. A latent Gaussian model with separate indicator and value dimensions represents sparsity patterns, correlations among active parameters, and the interactions between the two, so sparsity patterns and active values are optimized jointly, hierarchy-free. We show that the latent parameters of this model are identifiable from observed samples, unlike in the missing-data settings where related constructions originate, and introduce practical amortized inversion-based estimators for them. The estimators accurately recover latent correlation structures, and on the Lunar Lander benchmark the resulting ZIG-EDA converges faster and reaches higher final returns than a dense Gaussian EDA, a hand-crafted sparse evolutionary algorithm, and an ad-hoc sparse EDA, while finding controllers with only a small fraction of parameters active.

Abstract: Self-play reinforcement learning has recently emerged as a way to train driving policies without any human data. It uses cheap, large-scale simulations to substitute expensive, large-scale human driving demonstrations. A key limitation of this approach is that policies trained through pure self-play can learn effective but alien driving conventions incompatible with people. Previous works attempt to mitigate such behavioral misalignments through extensive reward engineering and domain randomization, which are brittle and labor-intensive. Instead of completely discarding human demonstrations, our method treats them as a regularization objective on top of a minimal safe goal-reaching reward. Like the spice in a good stew, we find that a little human data goes a long way: our method uses only 30 minutes of human demonstrations, 2500x fewer than comparable imitation learning approaches. ### [149] [ProMUSE: Progressive Multi-modal Uncertainty-guided Staged Evidential Alzheimer Disease Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19371)

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 ProMUSE 模型，通过评估临床数据的预测不确定性，智能决定是否需要进一步获取昂贵的 MRI/PET 影像，在大幅减少医疗检查开支的前提下实现了阿尔茨海默病的高效精准诊断。

Motivation: 阿尔茨海默病早期诊断至关重要，但 MRI 和 PET 等多模态影像检查成本高昂且难以普及，导致临床实践中全模态数据获取不切实际。因此，需要开发一种能根据需要动态调整模态需求、在保证精度的同时降低成本的方法。

Method: 提出了一种名为 ProMUSE 的渐进式多模态不确定性引导分阶段证据网络。该方法首先利用低成本临床数据进行基于狄利克雷分布的证据分类，量化不确定性；当不确定性超过阈值时，系统会逐步引入 MRI 或 PET 特征，并利用 Dempster-Shafer 理论对模态间的信念和不确定性进行融合。

Result: 在 ADNI、AIBL 和 OASIS 数据集的多个诊断任务中，ProMUSE 在实现与全模态基准模型相当或更优准确率的同时，减少了 50%-90% 的 MRI/PET 使用量，实现了显著的成本节约。

Conclusion: ProMUSE 为阿尔茨海默病（AD）的早期诊断提供了一种实用、具备不确定性感知且资源高效的解决方案，证明了通过自适应、分阶段引入昂贵模态可以显著降低临床筛查成本，同时保持高诊断精度。

Abstract: Alzheimer's disease (AD) is a fatal disorder that destroys memory and cognitive skills in the elderly population. Most treatments for AD are effective in the early stage, leading to an increasing demand for early AD diagnosis. AD diagnosis increasingly relies on multimodal data such as clinical assessments, structural Magnetic Resonance Imaging (MRI), and Positron Emission Tomography (PET) imaging. However, MRI and PET acquisition remain costly and not universally accessible, making full-modality inference impractical in real-world clinical workflows. We propose ProMUSE, a Progressive Multi-modal Uncertainty Guided Staged Evidential Network that adaptively determines when additional modalities are necessary, helping reduce the overall cost of data acquisition while maintaining accuracy. ProMUSE first performs evidential classification using low-cost clinical data and quantifies uncertainty via a Dirichlet-based subjective logic model. When uncertainty exceeds a learned threshold, ProMUSE progressively incorporates MRI or PET features, fusing modality-wise belief and uncertainty through Dempster-Shafer theory to obtain a calibrated multimodal prediction. This staged acquisition strategy enables accurate diagnosis while minimizing reliance on expensive imaging. Experiments on ADNI, AIBL, and OASIS across CN-AD, CN-MCI, and MCI-AD tasks demonstrate that ProMUSE achieves competitive or superior accuracy compared to full-modality baselines while reducing MRI/PET usage by 50-90%, yielding substantial cost savings. These results highlight ProMUSE as a practical, uncertainty-aware, and resource-efficient solution for real-world AD screening.

Existing methods require retraining each target without the ability to transfer knowledge across multiple VTs within the same patient or across patients. This is made possible by a task-agnostic surrogate neural network that learns the mapping from pacing sites to 12-lead ECG morphology, an active-learning strategy that refines this surrogate model by selecting the most informative pacing site for each target, and a continual learning strategy to do so sequentially while retaining knowledge from prior targets. Evaluated on an in-silico testbed consisting of sequentially-presented localization tasks across different physiological conditions and ventricular geometries, cAPM with and without replay of past data samples achieved an 81% probability of localizing within clinical tolerance (5 mm accuracy) using 4.5 pace-mapping sites, compared to the state-of-the-art active-learning method achieving 38% probability using 13.7 pacing sites. Abstract: Identifying anisotropic yield functions remains challenging since yielding is not directly observed in full-field mechanical measurements, directional calibration can require many loading directions, and selecting an appropriate analytical form is nontrivial. This study proposes a physics-informed framework for discovering yield functions from full-field displacement data and reaction force data, without stress observations, plastic strain measurements, direct yield surface data, or a prescribed parametric yield function. The framework identifies the yield function as a mechanically constrained constitutive component inside elastoplastic stress integration, rather than through direct stress-space supervision. The yield function is represented by a convex neural network that enforces convexity and positive homogeneity of degree one while imposing the assumed tension-compression symmetry, and this neural yield function is trained with a differentiable stress update and a physics-informed force equilibrium loss across multiple loading cases. The proposed framework is validated using finite element (FE) benchmark studies with von Mises, Hill 1948, and Yld2000-2d yield functions, assessing yield contour agreement, displacement-noise sensitivity, identifiability through plastically active stress states, epistemic uncertainty, and polynomial-surrogate deployment. In this study, we propose a hybrid GNN--FEM framework for efficient and generalizable phase-field fracture modeling. While phase-field approaches provide a robust variational framework for simulating complex crack evolution, their high computational cost limits practical applications because they require solving coupled, nonlinear, and history-dependent systems within an incremental finite element procedure. To address this challenge, a graph neural network surrogate is integrated into the conventional staggered scheme, replacing the phase-field update at each load increment while retaining the FEM-based displacement solver to enforce mechanical equilibrium and boundary conditions. ### [156] [How Linear Is a Transformer Feed-Forward Block? Per-Block Linear Recoverability Is Learned, Not Architectural](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19379)
*Stuart Whipp*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种量化Transformer FFN模块线性程度的方法（R^2_lin），研究发现FFN的线性度是学到的特性而非架构特性，且表现出显著的异构性，该指标可用于指导高效的模型压缩与分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Transformer的前馈神经网络（FFN）通常被视为非线性计算存储器，但目前缺乏对其非线性程度的量化测量。本文旨在探究FFN块的线性度，并理解这种特性在不同模型深度和架构下的演变规律。

Method: 研究者将每个FFN模块视为逐位置的输入到输出映射，通过闭式最小二乘法将其拆解为线性近似项和非线性残差项。通过计算线性近似项解释的方差比例（R^2_lin），量化每个模块的线性程度，并对比了GPT-2、Pythia-160m和llama-160m等模型在不同深度的表现。

Result: 研究发现：1. 线性度在模型深度上呈现高度异构且非单调的分布；2. 线性度并非由激活函数决定，而是由训练学到的属性；3. 难以通过简单的低秩双线性探针恢复残差，表明残差包含复杂的非线性结构；4. 该指标可作为有效的压缩引导，线性度高的模块可被大幅压缩。

Conclusion: FFN的线性可恢复性（R^2_lin）是模型学习到的属性，而非架构属性。该指标不仅揭示了模型内部非线性的分布规律，还可以作为模型压缩和模型理解的重要工具，有效识别可替换的线性模块并规避风险。

Abstract: Transformer feed-forward networks (FFNs) are often treated as nonlinear stores of computation, yet how nonlinear a trained FFN block actually is has rarely been measured. We treat each FFN as a position-wise input-to-output map and split it into the exact least-squares linear approximation plus a residual. The held-out variance the closed-form linear map explains defines a block's linear recoverability (R^2_lin), an optimiser-free measure of its linearity.
  Across all twelve blocks of GPT-2, Pythia-160m, and llama-160m, R^2_lin is highly heterogeneous and non-monotone with depth, ranging from near-linear (>0.99) to strongly nonlinear (<0.3) between adjacent blocks, and is not set by the activation function: same-width GELU models GPT-2 and Pythia-160m have sharply different profiles, so recoverability is a learned property of individual trained blocks, not an architectural one. A low-rank bilinear probe of the residual recovers only a few points of R^2, with gain uncorrelated with residual nonlinearity: the unrecovered computation is not a single position-wise product but higher-order or distributed structure.
  The measurement also serves as a targeted compression signal: recoverable blocks admit large single-layer replacements (GPT-2's early FFN at 8x fewer parameters for +0.77 perplexity), while low-recoverability blocks flag where this is unsafe. It further exposes a methodological pitfall: trained linear baselines can badly under-converge on ill-conditioned transformer activations, so we report the exact closed-form least-squares ceiling throughout.

</details>


### [157] [VERITAS: Verifier-Guided Proof Search for Zero-Shot Formal Theorem Proving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19399)
*Manish Acharya,Zhenyu Liao,Yueke Zhang,Kevin Leach,Yu Huang,Yifan Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: VERITAS 是一种旨在提升 LLM 形式化证明能力的新框架，它通过将详细的验证器反馈信息（而非仅二进制结果）引入两阶段的 MCTS 搜索过程，大幅提高了定理证明的成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型（LLM）的形式化验证方法往往只将复杂的验证器信号简化为二元的“通过/失败”结果，导致丢失了大量有价值的调试信息，从而限制了模型在复杂定理证明任务中的性能。

Method: 提出了一种两阶段协议 VERITAS：第一阶段使用 Best-of-N 采样进行初始探索；第二阶段利用第一阶段产生的错误信号（如语法错误、类型不匹配等）作为负例，通过评论家引导的 MCTS 进行深入的反馈驱动探索。

Result: VERITAS 在 miniF2F 基准测试上达到了 40.6% 的准确率（优于 Best-of-5 的 36.9% 和 Portfolio 的 26.2%），并在新发布的 VERITAS-CombiBench 上达到了 7.3%，证明了该方法在需要迭代检索引理名称的复杂任务中具有显著优势。

Conclusion: VERITAS 证明了通过将详细的验证器反馈整合到蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）中，可以显著提升大语言模型在形式化验证任务中的表现，证明了相比于简单的采样方法，利用细粒度反馈进行迭代式探索更具优势。

Abstract: LLM-based formal provers often collapse rich verifier signals (syntax errors, type mismatches, partial goal progress) into a binary pass/fail bit. We present VERITAS, a zero-shot framework that routes every verifier signal back into proof search through a two-phase protocol: Best-of-N sampling first, then a critic-guided MCTS pass that ingests Phase 1 failures as explicit negative examples. The protocol preserves every theorem solved by its own Phase 1 sweep, so Phase 2's additional solves are attributable to feedback-driven exploration. VERITAS reaches 40.6% on miniF2F (vs. an independently run Best-of-5 at 36.9%, Portfolio 26.2%) and 7.3% on VERITAS-CombiBench, a 55-theorem combinatorics benchmark we release on which Best-of-5 (1.8%) falls below Portfolio (3.6%), exposing that unguided sampling hurts when correct lemma names must be recovered iteratively from verifier feedback. Artifacts are available on GitHub.

</details>


### [158] [Thermodynamic Signatures of Reasoning: Free-Energy and Spectral-Form-Factor Diagnostics for Hallucination Detection in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19404)
*Salim Khazem*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种基于热力学势和随机矩阵理论的注意力谱描述符（Fes），用于在无需模型更新的情况下高效检测大型语言模型的幻觉，其性能显著优于现有的谱分析基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的基于注意力拉普拉斯算子的幻觉检测方法大多仅使用少数特征值或标量，未能充分利用整个谱结构的丰富信息。为了挖掘注意力谱中蕴含的推理质量信号，需要更全面、理论基础更扎实的谱描述符来提升检测性能。

Method: 1. 提出“自由能特征”（Fes）：将每一层的注意力拉普拉斯算子视为哈密顿量，提取其热力学势（配分函数、自由能、谱熵、热容量）以及随机矩阵理论中的谱形状因子。2. 理论分析：证明了Fes在注意力扰动下的Lipschitz稳定性、表达能力的完备性以及针对训练无关检测器的PAC边界。3. 实验验证：在6个模型和6个基准上评估，并采用轻量级探测器进行分类，同时对比了有监督和完全无监督（基于RMT偏差）的检测效果。

Result: 1. 在6个LLM模型和6个基准测试中，Fes探测器取得了最强的综合AUROC表现，平均比LapEig高出6.5个百分点，比GoR-4高出2.4个百分点。2. 在完全无监督设置下，基于RMT偏差评分的检测器达到了0.71的平均AUROC。3. 揭示了正确回答与幻觉在统计特性上的显著差异：前者更接近Wigner-Dyson统计，后者更接近泊松统计。

Conclusion: 该研究证明了“自由能特征”（Fes）作为一种无需微调的幻觉检测工具的有效性。它不仅在数学上具备稳定性和表达能力，还在实证中证明了基于统计物理和随机矩阵理论的方法能够捕捉LLM生成质量的深刻规律。研究揭示了模型生成过程中的统计特性差异：正确生成倾向于符合Wigner-Dyson分布，而幻觉则倾向于泊松分布。

Abstract: Hallucination detection in large language models (LLMs) is deployment-critical, and recent work shows that the spectrum of attention-derived graph Laplacians carries strong signal about reasoning quality. Prior spectral diagnostics, however, summarize the Laplacian spectrum by a handful of eigenvalues or hand-picked scalars, leaving most of its structure unused. We propose Free-Energy Signatures (Fes), a spectral descriptor that treats each layer's attention Laplacian as a Hamiltonian and extracts its thermodynamic potentials partition function, free energy, spectral entropy, heat capacity together with the random-matrix-theory (RMT) spectral form factor. We prove three results: (i)~Lipschitz stability of Fes under attention perturbation; (ii)~an expressiveness result showing that Fes enriches finite spectral summaries and approximates moment-derived spectral functionals under explicit regularity and grid-resolution assumptions; and (iii)~a finite-sample PAC bound on the AUROC of a training-free detector built from Fes. Empirically, across six open-weight LLMs and six benchmarks, a lightweight probe on Fes descriptors achieves the strongest aggregate AUROC among attention-spectral baselines, improving over LapEig by $+6.5$ AUROC points and over GoR-4 by $+2.4$ points on average, while requiring no update to the underlying LLM. In the fully unsupervised setting, an RMT-deviation score achieves mean AUROC $0.71$, providing a label-free but weaker detector. A complementary RMT analysis shows that correct generations exhibit more Wigner-Dyson like spectral statistics, whereas hallucinations exhibit more Poisson-like statistics. The anonymized code and config are provided in the supplementary material.

### [159] [FlexLAM: Resolving the Bottleneck Trade-off in Latent Action Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19408)
*Takanori Yoshimoto,Yang Hu,Naruya Kondo,Tatsuya Matsushima*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: FlexLAM 通过嵌套 Dropout 实现变长潜空间动作编码，解决了传统模型固定瓶颈的性能权衡问题，实现了推理时的灵活伸缩与更优的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的潜空间动作模型（LAMs）普遍采用固定容量的瓶颈设计，导致在处理动作对齐任务时存在两难：编码过紧会丢失关键动作线索，而编码过松则会引入过多冗余噪声，难以在稀疏标签下进行有效优化。

Method: 提出了 FlexLAM 模型，通过嵌套 Dropout（nested dropout）机制实现变长潜空间动作表示，使得模型能够生成“前缀有效”的编码；该方法无需更改现有架构或引入复杂损失函数，允许在推理阶段根据需要动态调整动作序列的长度（即 Token 预算）。

Result: 实验表明，FlexLAM 在多个基准测试中表现优于固定容量的 LAMs，并在相同 Token 预算下提供了更好的重建质量和对齐能力；此外，该模型支持在不重新训练的情况下动态调整推理精度，并在 Ego4D 数据集上提升了动作转换的重建效果。

Conclusion: FlexLAM 证明了变长潜空间动作是固定容量瓶颈的理想替代方案，不仅能够在推理时灵活调整精度，还能在相同的资源预算下提升特征表达能力，是视频驱动决策任务中的通用升级模块。

Abstract: Latent actions provide a compact interface between action-free video and downstream decision-making, yet existing Latent Action Models (LAMs) force every transition through a fixed-capacity bottleneck. We identify a bottleneck trade-off: overly tight codes can discard transition cues needed for action alignment, while overly loose codes preserve additional transition variation that must be resolved when alignment labels are scarce or narrowly distributed. FlexLAM replaces this fixed capacity with variable-length latent actions trained by nested dropout, yielding prefix-valid codes that capture compact transition structure first and add detail only when needed, without new architectures or losses. A single FlexLAM matches or surpasses separately trained fixed-capacity LAMs at every evaluated token budget under standard scarce-label supervision and under a low-return single-task alignment stress test, indicating that FlexLAM is not merely adjustable at inference time but learns a better latent-action interface at the same token budgets. The same model supports inference-time token-budget adjustment without retraining, and FlexLAM improves Ego4D transition reconstruction. These results suggest that variable-length latent actions are an architecture-free, drop-in upgrade to the fixed-capacity bottleneck in latent action models, latent-action world models, and video-pretrained action interfaces.

### [160] [Spectral DPPs via NEPv: A Scalable Continuous Relaxation of Determinantal MAP for Diversity-Aware Data Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19411)
*Richard Yi Da Xu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对大规模数据集下DPP-MAP求解困难的问题，本文提出了一种基于Stiefel流形松弛和非线性特征值问题（NEPv）的近线性时间求解算法（DPP-NEPv），有效提升了数据多样性筛选的扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 行列式点过程（DPP）是衡量多样性的重要数学工具，但其MAP（最大后验概率）目标函数属于NP-hard问题。传统的贪婪算法和采样算法在处理包含数百万至数十亿条数据的现代机器学习场景时，计算成本过于昂贵，难以满足大规模数据筛选的需求。

Method: 1. 将离散的DPP-MAP子集选择问题松弛为Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题；
2. 推导出一类具有特征向量依赖性的非线性特征值问题（NEPv）；
3. 提出一种基于自洽场（SCF）迭代的求解算法，该算法仅依赖于核函数的矩阵-向量乘法，计算复杂度达到近线性时间复杂度 O((ndk+nk^2)t)。

Result: 理论分析表明，所提出的SCF迭代算法具有基于谱隙（spectral-gap）的局部收缩保证。该方法成功实现了在接近线性时间复杂度下求解大规模DPP-MAP问题，适用于低秩核和特征映射核，从而有效解决了数据中心型AI中高维度、大规模样本的多样性筛选难题。

Conclusion: 通过将DPP-MAP转化为Stiefel流形上的连续优化问题，作者提出了一种高效的NEPv求解器。该方法摆脱了传统DPP算法对大规模数据集的计算瓶颈，为超大规模数据集的子集选择提供了理论基础和可扩展的算法框架。

Abstract: Selecting a small, diverse, high-quality subset from a massive pool of candidates is a recurring primitive in modern machine learning -- data curation and coreset selection for training and fine-tuning large models, active-learning batch acquisition, prompt and exemplar selection for in-context learning, retrieval diversification, and experimental design. Determinantal Point Processes (\DPP s) give a principled, well-calibrated notion of diversity for this task, but their \emph{MAP} objective -- pick a size-$k$ subset $S$ maximizing $\logdet(L_S)$ -- is NP-hard, and the standard greedy and sampling algorithms scale superlinearly in the ground-set size $n$. This cost is prohibitive precisely in the data-centric regime where diversity matters most, where $n$ ranges over millions to billions of candidate examples, features, or embeddings. We recast \DPP-MAP as a continuous optimization problem over the Stiefel manifold, and show that its first-order optimality conditions form a \emph{Nonlinear Eigenvalue Problem with eigenvector dependency} (\NEPv) of a previously unstudied form. This \NEPv\ admits a self-consistent field (\SCF) iteration with a spectral-gap-based local contraction guarantee, giving a principled iterative solver where the diversity objective drives an eigenvector-dependent operator. The resulting algorithm, \OurMethod, requires only matrix-vector products with the kernel and runs in time $O\!\big((ndk+nk^2)\,t\big)$ for a small number of iterations $t$, scaling near-linearly in $n$ and integrating directly with low-rank and feature-map kernels common in ML. This paper focuses on the relaxation, solver, and scaling analysis; full real-data benchmarking is left to a planned empirical study.

</details>


### [161] [Spectral Retrieval-Augmented Time-Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19412)
*Huu Hiep Nguyen,Minh Hoang Nguyen,Dung Nguyen,Hung Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: SpecReTF 是一种新型时间序列检索增强预测方法，通过综合频率域特征（幅度和相位）与指数加权的时间近期性，克服了现有方法在非平稳序列预测中的不足，显著提升了预测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的时间序列预测方法难以捕捉复杂且非平稳的模式；而现有的检索增强方法存在“频谱盲区”（忽略频率域的周期性特征）以及“时间近期性”缺失（未能区分近期与远期数据的权重）的问题。

Method: 提出了一种名为 SpecReTF 的检索方法：首先将时间序列转换为窗口化频率表示；其次，利用结合幅度和相位信息的指标计算相似度；最后，采用指数移动平均（EMA）加权方案，在增强历史模式的同时赋予近期数据更高的权重。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的实验结果表明，SpecReTF 显著优于传统的时域检索方法，在处理各类非平稳时间序列时展现出了更卓越的预测准确性。

Conclusion: SpecReTF 通过将频率域分析引入检索增强预测，并结合加权机制平衡历史模式与近期趋势，有效提升了复杂非平稳时间序列的预测精度，证明了频率信息与时效性在时间序列检索中的重要性。

Abstract: Time series forecasting leverages historical patterns to predict future values, but traditional methods face challenges when dealing with complex, non-stationary patterns that are difficult to memorize during training. Retrieval-augmented approaches have emerged as promising solutions by retrieving similar historical patterns to enhance predictions. However, existing retrieval methods suffer from two fundamental limitations: spectral blindness, which overlooks critical frequency-domain characteristics that capture underlying periodic structures, and temporal recency, which treats all historical data equally without emphasizing recent, more relevant patterns. In this paper, we propose SpecReTF, a novel retrieval method that addresses these issues by converting time series into windowed frequency representations, measuring similarity with a combined metric that captures both amplitude and phase information. To balance recency and historical context, we apply an exponential moving average weighting scheme that emphasizes recent windows. Extensive experiments on benchmark datasets demonstrate that SpecReTF outperforms time-domain retrieval methods, achieving superior forecasting accuracy across diverse, non-stationary time series.

### [162] [Does Text Actually Help? Uncovering and Resolving Text Collapse in Multimodal Time Series Forecasting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19413)
*Huu Hiep Nguyen,Minh Hoang Nguyen,Dung Nguyen,Hung Le*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 针对多模态时间序列预测中模型往往忽略文本分支的“文本坍缩”问题，本文提出了 REST-TS 框架，通过让文本分支专门预测数值支路的预测误差（残差），有效增强了文本模态的利用率，实现了更优的预测性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有将数值序列与文本报告结合的时间序列预测框架存在“文本坍缩”（Text Collapse）现象，即文本分支往往被忽略，退化为与输入无关的转换。这是由于数值序列本身具有强自相关性，导致模型在训练中过度依赖数值支路，而未能有效挖掘文本中蕴含的互补性世界知识。

Method: 提出了 REST-TS（基于残差的文本独占监督）框架。该方法的核心是将数值主干与文本分支解耦：数值分支先独立进行预测，而文本分支被明确设定为仅对数值预测产生的“残差”（即数值模型无法解释的部分）进行监督学习。这种设计消除了数值支路对文本支路的“遮蔽效应”，迫使文本模型提取真实的语义特征。

Result: 在多个真实领域的数据集和不同架构的主干模型上，REST-TS 均达到了最先进（SOTA）的性能水平。实验结果表明，该方法不仅显著提升了预测精度，而且有效提高了文本分支的利用率，证明了残差监督策略能迫使模型提取到有效的文本内容。

Conclusion: 通过强制文本分支专注于预测残差，REST-TS 有效解决了多模态时间序列预测中普遍存在的“文本坍缩”问题，证明了该设计范式能迫使模型充分利用文本模态中的互补信息，从而提升预测的准确性和鲁棒性。

Abstract: Multimodal time series forecasting, which pairs numerical sequences with domain-relevant textual reports, promises to inject world knowledge into forecasting pipelines. However, we uncover a critical failure mode in existing frameworks that we term text collapse: the text branch converges to a content-independent transformation, contributing negligible discriminative signal regardless of the input description. We argue that text collapse is a consequence of a fundamental asymmetry in time series forecasting: the numerical input is strongly autocorrelated with the output, making the numerical backbone inherently dominant, while the text branch, despite carrying complementary and often critical information, is insufficiently utilized, leading to its systematic underexploitation. To address this, we propose \textbf{REST-TS} (\textbf{R}esidual-\textbf{E}xclusive \textbf{S}upervision for \textbf{T}ext in \textbf{T}ime \textbf{S}eries), which turns the asymmetry into a design principle: the numerical backbone produces its own independent numerical forecast, and the text branch is exclusively supervised to predict the structured components of the residual, the prediction gap that numbers cannot explain. Because no numerical pathway can reduce these losses, the text branch must extract genuine content from the input description. Evaluated across diverse real-world domains and backbone architectures, REST-TS achieves state-of-the-art performance and consistently demonstrates greater text-branch utilization than existing frameworks, providing strong empirical evidence that supervising the text branch on the residual compels it to extract genuine content from the input.

</details>

### [164] [3D-DLP: Self-Supervised 3D Object-Centric Scene Representation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19451)
*Ellina Zhang,Madhaven Iyengar,Amir Zadeh,Chuan Li,Deepak Pathak,David Held,Tal Daniel*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该模型基于深度潜在粒子（DLP）框架，将场景级的 RGB-D 或体素观测分解为一组 3D 潜在粒子。每个粒子包含 3D 关键点位置、包围盒维度和外观特征等解耦属性，通过端到端的自监督重构目标进行训练，实现对场景的物体级分割。

Result: 实验表明，3D-DLP 在模拟和真实世界数据集中均表现出良好的可解释性和可控性，支持通过操纵粒子位置生成新场景。在机器人操纵任务中，相比基准模型，使用 3D-DLP 粒子表征显著提升了性能。

Conclusion: 3D-DLP 成功将 3D 场景分解为可解释的、紧凑的粒子表示，证明了基于物体中心（object-centric）的表征学习在机器人操纵任务中的有效性和优越性，为处理复杂 3D 场景提供了一种高效的范式。

Abstract: We introduce 3D-DLP, a self-supervised object-centric representation learning model that decomposes scene-level RGB-D or voxel observations into a set of 3D latent particles. Building on the Deep Latent Particles (DLP) framework, each particle encodes disentangled attributes, including 3D keypoint position, bounding box dimensions, and appearance features, and represents a distinct entity in the scene. The model learns interpretable per-particle segmentation maps through an end-to-end self-supervised reconstruction objective. We demonstrate on both simulated and real-world datasets that the learned latent space is interpretable and controllable: by manipulating particle positions and decoding, we can generate novel scene configurations. Furthermore, we show that leveraging these compact 3D latent particles for downstream robotic manipulation improves performance over baselines that either lack explicit 3D information or rely on memory-intensive dense 3D inputs without object-centric structure. Code and videos are available at https://eubooks3003.github.io/3d-dlp.

</details>


### [165] [Can In-Context Learning Support Intrinsic Curiosity?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.19476)
*Eric Elmoznino,Sangnie Bhardwaj,Johannes von Oswald,Rajai Nasser,Blaise Agüera y Arcas,João Sacramento,Rif A. Saurous,Guillaume Lajoie*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出利用大模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力来替代传统的昂贵梯度更新，从而高效计算“学习进度”并驱动智能体进行自动化数据探索，成功解决了好奇心驱动探索在高计算成本下的实用性瓶颈。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的基于“学习进度”的内在好奇心机制通常需要昂贵的内部梯度下降更新循环来评估模型提升，这在计算上限制了其在大规模场景中的应用。研究者旨在探索序列模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力是否能够替代昂贵的梯度更新，从而实现高效的自动化数据选择。

Method: 研究团队提出了利用预训练序列模型的上下文学习（ICL）能力作为“世界模型”，通过观察预测误差和反事实上下文操作，计算无需梯度下降更新的内在奖励（intrinsic rewards）来驱动智能体探索。研究首先在理论上证明了在通用马尔可夫决策过程中该方法的偏差不可避免，随后证明了在非时间性设置（如主动学习）下，ICL导出的奖励能够收敛于真实学习进度，并通过连续与符号化环境的实验进行了验证。

Result: 理论证明显示，在一般马尔可夫决策过程中，基于ICL的奖励估计存在无法消除的偏差或实现局限；但在主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计等非时间性子类中，ICL奖励可以作为真实学习进度的有效界限并渐进收敛。实验结果证实，该框架能够成功训练出具备最优探索能力的好奇数据收集策略。

Conclusion: 本研究表明，利用上下文学习（ICL）作为无需梯度更新的世界模型来度量“学习进度”在理论上存在边界。虽然在马尔可夫决策过程中存在本质偏差，但在主动学习和贝叶斯实验设计等非时间性子类问题中，ICL导出的奖励能够有效逼近真实学习进度，为实现高效、自动化的数据选择提供了新路径。

Abstract: Effective machine learning depends not only on how we model data, but also on what data we choose to collect. While large sequence models have revolutionized data modeling, the problem of automated data selection, or "intrinsic curiosity", remains a significant challenge. Classic approaches incentivize exploration by rewarding an agent based on its "learning progress", which measures how much a newly acquired observation improves a world model's predictive ability. However, evaluating these rewards traditionally requires expensive inner loops of gradient descent updates within each trajectory, rendering them computationally impractical at scale. In this work, we investigate whether the emergent in-context learning (ICL) capabilities of sequence models can eliminate this bottleneck by serving as immediate, update-free world models. Specifically, we evaluate whether an exploration policy can be trained to maximize learning progress, using solely the prediction errors and counterfactual context manipulations of an in-context learner. We first prove that in general Markov decision processes, this is in fact impossible in an unbiased way: the resulting intrinsic rewards either suffer from nuisance terms that bias their estimation of true learning progress, or they cannot be implemented using an in-context learner's prediction errors. Conversely, we prove a positive result for a broad subclass of non-temporal settings, encompassing active learning and Bayesian Experimental Design: here, ICL-derived rewards successfully bound and asymptotically converge to the true learning progress. We corroborate our theory with controlled experiments across continuous and symbolic environments, demonstrating that our ICL-driven framework successfully trains curious data-collection policies that explore optimally.

</details>

*Thomas Frost,Steve Harris*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 该论文推出了 Insulin4RL，这是一个基于 MIMIC-IV 构建的医疗离线强化学习数据集，其独特之处在于保留了真实临床轨迹中不规则的时间输入与动作，旨在解决传统离散化处理造成的临床现实性缺失问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>
